Now try a repeating-key XOR cipher. E.g. it should take a string â€œhello worldâ€ and, given the key is â€œkeyâ€, xor the first letter â€œhâ€ with â€œkâ€, then xor â€œeâ€ with â€œeâ€, then â€œlâ€ with â€œyâ€, and then xor next char â€œlâ€ with â€œkâ€ again, then â€œoâ€ with â€œeâ€ and so on. You may use an index of coincidence, Hamming distance, Kasiski examination, statistical tests or whatever method you feel would show the best result.
